 com / eymxhrr6je In the second phase of Lok Sabha elections 2019, votes will be cast on 10 Lok Sabha seats in Maharashtra on 18 April
 inamen buldhaana, akola, amravati, hingoli, nanded, parabhani, bid, osmanabad, latur or sholapur seat shaamil he
 In terms of 2014, five of these 10 seats are occupied by BJP
 jabaki shivasena ke teen or congress ke do saansad hai
 Instead of this time, in the political equation, it is being considered as a contest between the Shiv sena-bjp and congress-ncp alliance, but the BSP and Prakash Ambedkar's party has made a triangular contest in many seats
 latur:latur loksabhaa seat se bijepi ne apane maujuuda saansad sunil gaekwad kaa tikat katkar sudhakar tukaraam shrangare ko utaara he
 While 10 candidates are in the fray including Congress Kamant Machindra, BSP Siddharth Kumar Digambarao Suryavanshi and the deprived Bahujan Aghadi Ram Garkar
 latur seat se congress ke shivaraj patil kii paramparaagat seat rahi he
 But the BJP had managed to make a dent in this area
 congress ise waapas laane ke liye kaamant machhindra par daanv khelaa he
 But the way BJP has brought down Shrangare by cutting the ticket of its current MP
 isse bijepi ko party ke andar or baahar donon chunautiyon se saamana karnaa pad rahaa he
 Buldhana: 12 candidates are in the fray for Buldhana Lok Sabha seat including Jadhav Prataprao Ganpatrao from Shiv Sena, Dr
 Rajendra Bhaskarwar Shingne from Congress and Abdul Hafeez Abdul Aziz from BSP
 mukhya muqabla bijepi or congress ke bich he
 Jadhav has been a BJP MP twice before, but this time Shiv Sena has played the stakes
 congress se utarane vaale shingane bhi ensipi se do baar isi seat se chunaav lard chuke hai
 Although he has not won
 akola:akola loksabhaa seat par congress se hidayatulla barkatullah patel, bijepi se dhotre sanjay shamrao or vanchit bahujan aghadi ke pramukh prakaash ambedkar sahit 11 pratyaashee maidan main hai
 The battle of Akola seat has become interesting with Prakash Ambedkar landing in the political arena
 unhen ovaisi kii party AIMIM kaa samarthan hasil he
 Dhotre of BJP won this seat in 2014
 is baar kaa siyaasi sangram trikoniya hoti najar aa rahi he
 Amravati: Amravati Lok Sabha seat is reserved for the scheduled castes, which is considered to be a strong fort of Shiv Sena
 pichley 25 saal se shivasena kaa is seat par kabja he
 Shiv Sena has also fielded its sitting MP Adsul Anandrao this time
 jabaki congress-ensipi gathbandhan main shaamil yuva swabhimaan party ke adhyaksh ravi rana kii patni navaneet cor rana ko utaara he
 The BSP has placed bets on Arun Wankhede and Bahujan Maha Party at Athawale Sanjay
 haalanki dilachasp baat ye he ki is seat par kabhi koi mahila chunaav nahin haari he, aise main gathbandhan ne shivasena ke jeet kaa silsilaa rokane ke liye navaneet cor rana par bharosa jataayaa he
 Hingoli: Congress has fielded Subhash Wankhede, who came from Shiv Sena, this time from Hingoli seat in Maharashtra, replacing his current MP Rajiv Satav
 jabaki shivasena ne hemanth patil, bispi ne dhanave datta or indian union muslim lig se altaaf ahamed sahit 17 pratyaashee maidan main he
 In the Modi wave too, the Congress had managed to win this seat
 is baar dalit or muslim voton ke bikharaav kii aas main shivasena jeet kii ummid lagaae hue hai
 Nanded: Nanded Lok Sabha seat is considered a strong stronghold of Congress
 nanded seat par congress ke pradesh adhyaksh or purv mukhyamantri ashok chavaan maidan main hai to bijepi ne chikhalikar pratap govindrav ko utaara he
 While SP Abdul Samad, deprived Bahujan Aghadi has announced Bhinge Yashpal Narasimha Rao, Bahujan Mukti Party has declared Mohan Anandrao as its candidate
 ashok chavaan ke grih kshetra hone ke naate bijepi is ilaake main camel khilaane se maharoom rahi he
 But the way the SP and Prakash Ambedkar's party have fielded candidates this time
 aise main bijepi is ilaake main jeet kii ummid lagaae hue he
 Parbhani: Parbhani Lok Sabha seat is counted among the strong seats of Shiv Sena
 is seat par shivasena ne apane maujuuda saansad sanjay haribhaau jadhav, ensipi ne rajesh uttam raav, basapa ne vaijanath seetaram or vanchit bahujan aghadi ne alamgir mohammad khan ko utraa he
 This time the NCP has placed a bet on a new face in place of its old candidate
 jabaki shivasena apane puraane chehre ke sahare jeet kii aas lagaae he
 Beed: The Beed seat of Maharashtra is considered a strong constituency of the BJP
 bijepi ne is par divangat gopinath munde kii beti preetam munde ko chunaav maidan main utaara he to vahiin ensipi ne bajrang manohar sonwane ko utaara he
 The underprivileged Bahujan Aghadi is contesting from Syed Muzammil Syed Jamil from Vishnu Jadhav and SP
 2014 main gopinath munde ne jeet darj kii thi, lekin unke nidhan ke baad unki beti ne raajnneetik viraasat ko sambhala tha
 This time in the changed political equation, there is a tough challenge for Gopinath Munde to take over the political legacy
 par sapa ke muslim ummidavaar ke utarane se preetam munde ek baar phir jeet kii ummid lagaae hai
 Osmanabad: On the Osmanabad Lok Sabha seat, Shiv Sena has cut the ticket of its sitting MP Omroj Nimbalkar, NCP has Ranjgit Singh Padmasinh Patil, BSP from Shivaji Pandharinath Oman and underprivileged Bahujan Aghadi in the Arjun constituency
 2014 main shivasena se ravindra gaekwad ne jeet darj kii thi
 The congress-ncp alliance has occupied this seat for a long time
 aise main modi lahar main shivasena ke dwaara jiti gai seat ko ensipi dobaaraa se waapas laane ke liye harsambhav koshish main juty he
 Solapur: The Solapur Lok Sabha seat has been a traditional constituency of veteran Congress leader and former Chief Minister Sushil Kumar Shinde, but in the Modi wave, the BJP managed to feed the lotus in this area
 is baar congress ne susheel kumaar scindia ko utaara he
 Whereas BJP replaced sitting MP Sharad Bansode with religious guru Jai Siddheshwar Shivacharya and underprivileged Bahujan Aghadi betting on Ambedkar Prakash Yashwant
 is seat par lingayat or dalit matadaata nirnayak bhoomika main he, jiskaa phayda uthaane ke liye bijepi ne siddheshwar shivacharya par bharosa jaataa he, lekin congress ke susheel kumaar scindia ke sahare ek baar phir vaapasi karnaa chaahati he
 Every news of the election will be received directly in your inbox
 aam chunaav kii tazaa khabaron se apadet rahane ke liesbscribakaren ajtak kaa ellection special newzlator In Chhindwara district of Madhya Pradesh, in a dispute over dyeing, an attempt was made to burn a girl alive by putting kerosene on her
 use gambheer haalat main aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya he
 Police have arrested the accused
 police ke anusaar ravivaar ko holi ke dauraan kudipura thane kii basant colony main sunil ne pados main rahane vaale ravi pradhan kii bahan par rang daal diya
 The color was mixed in hot water
 is baat ko lekar donon pakshon main vivaad bad gaya

 ab aadhikarik taur par piem modi ne iske khilaaf muhim ched di he
 But the question is what is single-use plastic and what plastic products come under its purview? Let's know the answer
 
 
 kya he single-yuj plastic?single-yuj plastic use kehete hai jiskaa ham ek baar hi istemaal karte hai
 In everyday life, there are many such plastic products that we throw away once
 isi tarah ke plastic ko single yuj plastic kaha jaataa he
 It is also known as disposable plastic
 single yuj plastic product kii baat karen to isamen- plastic bag, plastic kii bottlen, straw, cap, plates, food packjing main istemaal hone vaale plastic, gift reppers or coffee ke dispojable kaps aadi shaamil hai
 E-commerce companies consume 40% of the e-commerce companies in India in single plastic use
 ek anumaan ke mutabik salanaa upyog hone vaale plastic product main kareeb 40 fisadi plastic kii khapat i-commers sector main hoti he

 Delhi Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal had said in the coming days to give relief to the Delhiites on the fix charge given with the electricity bill
 kejariwal ne kaha tha ki wo agle maheene bijli companiyon se janata ke liye fiks charge ko ghataane kii maang karenge, jisase dilliwaalon ko apane bijli bill main badi kami dekhne ko milegi
 But Delhi BJP has attacked this announcement of Kejriwal in reverse
 bijepi netaa manoj tiwari ne aarope lagaate hue kaha ki bijli half pani maaf ke naare ke saath dilli kii satta main aae arvind kejariwal ab bijli ke fiks charge badhaakar bijli companiyon ke saath milakar dilli ke logon ko lut rahe hai
 Responding strongly to Kejriwal's announcement, Delhi Pradesh President of the Bharatiya Janata Party Manoj Tiwari said that last year when the Delhi government had increased the fix charge, even after registering an objection, we had said that Kejriwal was deliberate to benefit the power companies
 Tax fixes are increasing the charge
 dilli bijepi ne or dilli kii tamaam aradblue ne iskaa virodh pichley saal bhi kiya tha, lekin kejariwal sarkaar ne manamaana ravaiya apanaate hue dilli kii janata ko thagne kaa kaam kiya
 In a press release issued by the Delhi BJP, it has been claimed that the power companies have benefited about 5 thousand crores this year after increasing the fix charge
 bijepi dilli adhyaksh manoj tiwari ne kaha ki bijli companiyon kii kejariwal sarkaar ke saath mileebhagat ke chalate dilli main fiks charge bade hai jiske kaaran logon ko manhagi bijli di ja rahi he
 Economic burden has increased due to expensive electricity
 aise main bijepi ne kejariwal sarkaar se fiks charge ke naam par ikaitha kiye gaye lagbhag 5 hajaar karod dilli kii janata ko jald se jald rifund karne kii maang kii he
 Kejriwal is making announcements about the elections- In a very sharp comment on BJP Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal, Delhi BJP President Manoj Tiwari said that Kejriwal, who announces new free scheme for the people of Delhi, has become a curse for the public

 However, it was claimed by Delhi Bijpi that after these announcements by Arvind Kejriwal, there would be no impact on Delhiites and Delhiites would remove Kejriwal from Delhi chair after next six months
